If you are truly so unhappy, and so ungrateful, for that matter ...please leave Youtube and get another job.  You are not in hell.  I could tell you what hell is, because I am actually there...but unlike you, I realize that even in my situation (which is more extreme than you could ever imagine)...there are things to be grateful for, and there is someone who is worse off than i am.  please stop with the "i hate my life, i hate my career, i hate Youtube, woe is me" business. I would give anything in the world to just go one month without a hospital stay and to be able to work again. i have been confined to my bed and in extreme pain, and mostly paralyzed, for 8 years. I watch your videos because you (used) to seem like someone who enjoyed their life, enjoyed their health (which is a blessing like you will never understand), and weren't the usual ungrateful shits that I encounter.   You will lose me as a follower if you continue the whining...which I'm sure you don't care about...but you're also losing your ability to claim that you're a decent human. Decent humans don't whine about their success to an audience that likely has much less than they do (in every way, of everything) and they are *grateful*. If I can think of twenty things in one day, that I am grateful for, with a life that literally no one would want, where i have lost absolutely everything that every mattered to me...you can be at least a little grateful for the fact that you have everything that people like me never will.   You're lucky that health problems don't happen to the people that deserve them, because they are so ungrateful and do not appreciate what they have. Instead, you will continue to take your life and body for granted, while I will continue to fight just to be able to one day leave my bed...and you will remain ungrateful, while the more I lose, the more grateful I am for what I have left. I've actually bought "flower ice cream" when I visited Paris, but it wasn't actually ice cream. The place I went to, called Amorino http://www.amorino.com/fr/boutiques.html , uses gelato instead of ice cream, which is understandably much more malleable and makes petal shaping much easier. So if you were to try this again, not saying you need to, I'd suggest using gelato. :)
